I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
OnnxScoringModel can't release resources until JVM is stopped
I've noticed that for `OnnxScoringModel`, there is no way to call `close()` that should be propagated to `OrtSession.close()`, which is responsible for releasing any non-jvm allocated memory allocated by OrtSession. When OnnxScoringModel is called multiple times, especially with larger models, it can allocate significant amount of memory and might cause machine swapping.

OnnxScoringModel doesn't implement AutoCloseable - will that be hard to add? Also, I think the above behavior should be documented, at least until `close()` is added.

</pr_description>

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring.onnx;
     2	
     3	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession;
     4	import dev.langchain4j.data.segment.TextSegment;
     5	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.Response;
     6	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.TokenUsage;
     7	import dev.langchain4j.model.scoring.ScoringModel;
     8	
     9	import java.util.List;
    10	import java.util.stream.Collectors;
    11	
    12	abstract class AbstractInProcessScoringModel implements ScoringModel {
    13	
    14	    public AbstractInProcessScoringModel() {
    15	    }
    16	
    17	    static OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder loadFromFileSystem(String pathToModel, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength, boolean normalize) {
    18	        try {
    19	            return new OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder(pathToModel, options, pathToTokenizer, modelMaxLength, normalize);
    20	        } catch (Exception e) {
    21	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
    22	        }
    23	    }
    24	
    25	    protected abstract OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder model();
    26	
    27	    public Response<List<Double>> scoreAll(List<TextSegment> segments, String query) {
    28	        OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder.ScoringAndTokenCount scoresAndTokenCount = this.model().scoreAll(query,
    29	                segments.stream().map(TextSegment::text).collect(Collectors.toList()));
    30	        return Response.from(scoresAndTokenCount.scores, new TokenUsage(scoresAndTokenCount.tokenCount));
    31	    }
    32	}

2026-05-30 02:48:01,240 - DEBUG - swea-tools-langchain4j__langchain4j-4876 - Retrieved state from environment: {}
2026-05-30 02:48:01,243 - INFO - swea-agent-langchain4j__langchain4j-4876 - 🤖 MODEL INPUT
OBSERVATION:

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring.onnx;
     2	
     3	import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.Encoding;
     4	import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.HuggingFaceTokenizer;
     5	import ai.djl.util.PairList;
     6	import ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor;
     7	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtEnvironment;
     8	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtException;
     9	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession;
    10	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession.Result;
    11	
    12	import java.nio.file.Paths;
    13	import java.util.*;
    14	
    15	import static ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor.createTensor;
    16	
    17	class OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder {
    18	
    19	    private final OrtEnvironment environment;
    20	    private final OrtSession session;
    21	    private final Set<String> expectedInputs;
    22	    private final HuggingFaceTokenizer tokenizer;
    23	    private final boolean normalize;
    24	
    25	    public OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder(String modelPath, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength, boolean normalize) {
    26	        try {
    27	            this.environment = OrtEnvironment.getEnvironment();
    28	            this.session = this.environment.createSession(modelPath, options);
    29	            this.expectedInputs = session.getInputNames();
    30	            Map<String, String> tokenizerOptions = new HashMap<String, String>() {{
    31	                put("padding", "true");
    32	                put("truncation", "LONGEST_FIRST"); // Default maximum length limit, LONGEST-FIRST prioritizes truncating the longest part
    33	                put("modelMaxLength", String.valueOf(modelMaxLength - 2));
    34	            }};
    35	            this.normalize = normalize;
    36	            this.tokenizer = HuggingFaceTokenizer.newInstance(Paths.get(pathToTokenizer), tokenizerOptions);
    37	        } catch (Exception e) {
    38	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
    39	        }
    40	    }
    41	
    42	    static class ScoringAndTokenCount {
    43	
    44	        List<Double> scores;
    45	        int tokenCount;
    46	
    47	        ScoringAndTokenCount(List<Double> scores, int tokenCount) {
    48	            this.scores = scores;
    49	            this.tokenCount = tokenCount;
    50	        }
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    ScoringAndTokenCount scoreAll(String query, List<String> documents) {
    54	        List<Double> scores;
    55	        int tokenCount = 0;
    56	        int queryTokenCount = tokenizer.tokenize(query).size() - 2;
    57	        PairList<String, String> pairs = new PairList<>();
    58	        for (String document : documents) {
    59	            pairs.add(query, document);
    60	            tokenCount += queryTokenCount + tokenizer.tokenize(document).size() - 2; // do not count special tokens [CLS] and [SEP]
    61	        }
    62	        try (Result result = this.encode(pairs)) {
    63	            scores = this.toScore(result);
    64	        } catch (OrtException e) {
    65	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
    66	        }
    67	        return new ScoringAndTokenCount(scores, tokenCount);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    private Result encode(PairList<String, String> pairs) throws OrtException {
    71	        Encoding[] encodings = this.tokenizer.batchEncode(pairs);
    72	        long[][] inputIds = new long[encodings.length][];
    73	        long[][] attentionMask = new long[encodings.length][];
    74	        long[][] tokenTypeIds = new long[encodings.length][];
    75	
    76	        for (int i = 0; i < encodings.length; i++) {
    77	            inputIds[i] = encodings[i].getIds();
    78	            attentionMask[i] = encodings[i].getAttentionMask();
    79	            tokenTypeIds[i] = encodings[i].getTypeIds();
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        try (
    83	                OnnxTensor inputIdsTensor = createTensor(environment, inputIds);
    84	                OnnxTensor attentionMaskTensor = createTensor(environment, attentionMask);
    85	                OnnxTensor tokenTypeIdsTensor = createTensor(this.environment, tokenTypeIds);
    86	        ) {
    87	            Map<String, OnnxTensor> inputs = new HashMap<>();
    88	            inputs.put("input_ids", inputIdsTensor);
    89	            inputs.put("attention_mask", attentionMaskTensor);
    90	
    91	            if (expectedInputs.contains("token_type_ids")) {
    92	                inputs.put("token_type_ids", tokenTypeIdsTensor);
    93	            }
    94	
    95	            return session.run(inputs);
    96	        }
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    private List<Double> toScore(OrtSession.Result result) throws OrtException {
   100	        float[][] output = (float[][]) result.get(0).getValue();
   101	        List<Double> scores = new ArrayList<>();
   102	        for (float[] floats : output) {
   103	            if (normalize) {
   104	                scores.add(sigmoid(floats[0]));
   105	            } else {
   106	                scores.add((double)floats[0]);
   107	            }
   108	        }
   109	        return scores;
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    private double sigmoid(float x) {
   113	        return 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-x));
   114	    }
   115	
   116	}

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring;
     2	
     3	import dev.langchain4j.data.segment.TextSegment;
     4	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.Response;
     5	
     6	import java.util.List;
     7	
     8	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.ValidationUtils.ensureEq;
     9	import static java.util.Collections.singletonList;
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * Represents a model capable of scoring a text against a query.
    13	 * <br>
    14	 * Useful for identifying the most relevant texts when scoring multiple texts against the same query.
    15	 * <br>
    16	 * The scoring model can be employed for re-ranking purposes.
    17	 */
    18	public interface ScoringModel {
    19	
    20	    /**
    21	     * Scores a given text against a given query.
    22	     *
    23	     * @param text  The text to be scored.
    24	     * @param query The query against which to score the text.
    25	     * @return the score.
    26	     */
    27	    default Response<Double> score(String text, String query) {
    28	        return score(TextSegment.from(text), query);
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    /**
    32	     * Scores a given {@link TextSegment} against a given query.
    33	     *
    34	     * @param segment The {@link TextSegment} to be scored.
    35	     * @param query   The query against which to score the segment.
    36	     * @return the score.
    37	     */
    38	    default Response<Double> score(TextSegment segment, String query) {
    39	        Response<List<Double>> response = scoreAll(singletonList(segment), query);
    40	        ensureEq(response.content().size(), 1,
    41	                "Expected a single score, but received %d", response.content().size());
    42	        return Response.from(response.content().get(0), response.tokenUsage(), response.finishReason());
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    /**
    46	     * Scores all provided {@link TextSegment}s against a given query.
    47	     *
    48	     * @param segments The list of {@link TextSegment}s to score.
    49	     * @param query    The query against which to score the segments.
    50	     * @return the list of scores. The order of scores corresponds to the order of {@link TextSegment}s.
    51	     */
    52	    Response<List<Double>> scoreAll(List<TextSegment> segments, String query);
    53	}

    70	    }

Let me look at the OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder more carefully. It creates an `OrtSession` and `OrtEnvironment`, neither of which are closed. The `OrtSession` has a `close()` method that should be called to release native resources.

Here's my plan:
1. Add a `close()` method to `OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder` that closes the `OrtSession`
2. Make `OnnxScoringModel` implement `AutoCloseable` and propagate `close()` to the encoder
3. Also consider making `AbstractInProcessScoringModel` implement `AutoCloseable` and/or `ScoringModel` extend `AutoCloseable`

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.gpullama3;
     2	
     3	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.AiMessage;
     4	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.ChatMessage;
     5	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.SystemMessage;
     6	import dev.langchain4j.data.message.UserMessage;
     7	import dev.langchain4j.model.chat.request.ChatRequest;
     8	import java.io.IOException;
     9	import java.lang.ref.Cleaner;
    10	import java.nio.file.Path;
    11	import java.util.ArrayList;
    12	import java.util.List;
    13	import java.util.Set;
    14	import java.util.function.IntConsumer;
    15	import org.beehive.gpullama3.auxiliary.LastRunMetrics;
    16	import org.beehive.gpullama3.inference.sampler.Sampler;
    17	import org.beehive.gpullama3.inference.state.State;
    18	import org.beehive.gpullama3.model.Model;
    19	import org.beehive.gpullama3.model.format.ChatFormat;
    20	import org.beehive.gpullama3.model.loader.ModelLoader;
    21	import org.beehive.gpullama3.tornadovm.TornadoVMMasterPlan;
    22	
    23	/**
    24	 * Abstract base class for GPULlama3 chat models providing core functionality for conversation management and token generation.
    25	 *
    26	 * <p>This class handles:
    27	 * <ul>
    28	 *   <li>Model initialization and configuration</li>
    29	 *   <li>Conversation state management (stateless approach)</li>
    30	 *   <li>Token encoding and decoding using proper chat formats</li>
    31	 *   <li>Both CPU and GPU execution modes</li>
    32	 *   <li>System and user message processing</li>
    33	 *   <li>Automatic resource cleanup using modern Cleaner API</li>
    34	 * </ul>
    35	 *
    36	 *
    37	 * <p>GPU resources are automatically cleaned up when the model is garbage collected,
    38	 * but can also be manually freed using {@link #freeTornadoVMGPUResources()} or
    39	 * {@link #close()}.
    40	 *
    41	 * <p>Subclasses should implement specific model interfaces (e.g., ChatModel or
    42	 * StreamingChatModel) while leveraging this base functionality.
    43	 */
    44	abstract class GPULlama3BaseModel implements AutoCloseable {
    45	    private static final Cleaner CLEANER = Cleaner.create();
    46	
    47	    private final Integer START_POSITION = 0;
    48	    State state;
    49	    List<Integer> promptTokens;
    50	    ChatFormat chatFormat;
    51	    TornadoVMMasterPlan tornadoVMPlan;
    52	    private Integer maxTokens;
    53	    private Boolean onGPU;
    54	    private Model model;
    55	    private Sampler sampler;
    56	    /** Cleaner for automatic resource management */
    57	    private Cleaner.Cleanable cleanable;
    58	    /** Flag to track if resources have been closed */
    59	    private boolean closed = false;
    60	
    61	    public void init(Path modelPath, Double temperature, Double topP, Integer seed, Integer maxTokens, Boolean onGPU) {
    62	        this.maxTokens = maxTokens;
    63	        this.onGPU = onGPU;
    64	
    65	        try {
    66	            this.model = ModelLoader.loadModel(modelPath, maxTokens, true, onGPU);
    67	            this.state = model.createNewState();
    68	            this.sampler = Sampler.selectSampler(
    69	                    model.configuration().vocabularySize(), temperature.floatValue(), topP.floatValue(), seed);
    70	
    71	            this.chatFormat = model.chatFormat();
    72	
    73	            if (onGPU) {
    74	                tornadoVMPlan = TornadoVMMasterPlan.initializeTornadoVMPlan(state, model);
    75	                // Register automatic cleanup with Cleaner
    76	                this.cleanable = CLEANER.register(this, new TornadoVMCleanupAction(tornadoVMPlan));
    77	            } else {
    78	                this.cleanable = null;
    79	            }
    80	        } catch (IOException e) {
    81	            throw new RuntimeException("Failed to load model from " + modelPath, e);
    82	        }
    83	    }
    84	    // @formatter:off
    85	
    86	    public Model getModel() {
    87	        return model;
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    public Sampler getSampler() {
    91	        return sampler;
    92	    }
    93	
    94	    /**
    95	     * Generates a chat response from the model.
    96	     * Used by GPULlama3StreamingChatModel.
    97	     * @param request
    98	     * @param tokenConsumer
    99	     * @return
   100	     */
   101	    public String modelResponse(ChatRequest request, IntConsumer tokenConsumer) {
   102	        this.promptTokens = new ArrayList<>();
   103	
   104	        if (model.shouldAddBeginOfText()) {
   105	            promptTokens.add(chatFormat.getBeginOfText());
   106	        }
   107	
   108	        processPromptMessages(request.messages());
   109	
   110	        Set<Integer> stopTokens = chatFormat.getStopTokens();
   111	        List<Integer> responseTokens;
   112	
   113	        if (onGPU) {
   114	            responseTokens = model.generateTokensGPU(
   115	                    state,
   116	                    START_POSITION,
   117	                    promptTokens.subList(START_POSITION, promptTokens.size()),
   118	                    stopTokens,
   119	                    maxTokens,
   120	                    sampler,
   121	                    false,
   122	                    tokenConsumer,
   123	                    tornadoVMPlan);
   124	        } else {
   125	            responseTokens = model.generateTokens(
   126	                    state,
   127	                    START_POSITION,
   128	                    promptTokens.subList(START_POSITION, promptTokens.size()),
   129	                    stopTokens,
   130	                    maxTokens,
   131	                    sampler,
   132	                    false,
   133	                    tokenConsumer);
   134	        }
   135	
   136	        Integer stopToken = null;
   137	        if (!responseTokens.isEmpty() && stopTokens.contains(responseTokens.getLast())) {
   138	            stopToken = responseTokens.getLast();
   139	            responseTokens.removeLast();
   140	        }
   141	
   142	        String responseText = model.tokenizer().decode(responseTokens);
   143	
   144	        // Add the response content tokens to conversation history
   145	        promptTokens.addAll(responseTokens);
   146	
   147	        // Add the stop token to complete the message
   148	        if (stopToken != null) {
   149	            promptTokens.add(stopToken);
   150	        }
   151	
   152	        if (stopToken == null) {
   153	            return "Ran out of context length...\n Increase context length with by passing to llama-tornado --max-tokens XXX";
   154	        } else {
   155	            return responseText;
   156	        }
   157	    }
   158	    // @formatter:on
   159	
   160	    public void printLastMetrics() {
   161	        LastRunMetrics.printMetrics();
   162	    }
   163	
   164	    /**
   165	     * Processes chat messages and encodes them into prompt tokens.
   166	     *
   167	     * <p>This method iterates through the provided chat messages and converts them into
   168	     * encoded tokens based on their message type and role. The encoded tokens are appended to the {@link #promptTokens} list for later use in model inference.
   169	     *
   170	     * <p>Supported message types:
   171	     * <ul>
   172	     *   <li>{@link UserMessage} - Encoded with the USER role</li>
   173	     *   <li>{@link SystemMessage} - Encoded with the SYSTEM role (only if {@link Model#shouldAddSystemPrompt()} returns true)</li>
   174	     *   <li>{@link AiMessage} - Encoded with the ASSISTANT role</li>
   175	     * </ul>
   176	     *
   177	     * <p>Each message is encoded using the configured {@link ChatFormat}, which ensures
   178	     * proper formatting according to the model's requirements (e.g., Llama 3 chat format).
   179	     *
   180	     * @param messageList
   181	     *         the list of chat messages to process and encode
   182	     * @see ChatFormat#encodeMessage(ChatFormat.Message)
   183	     * @see UserMessage
   184	     * @see SystemMessage
   185	     * @see AiMessage
   186	     */
   187	    private void processPromptMessages(List<ChatMessage> messageList) {
   188	        for (ChatMessage msg : messageList) {
   189	            if (msg instanceof UserMessage userMessage) {
   190	                promptTokens.addAll(chatFormat.encodeMessage(
   191	                        new ChatFormat.Message(ChatFormat.Role.USER, userMessage.singleText())));
   192	            } else if (msg instanceof SystemMessage systemMessage && model.shouldAddSystemPrompt()) {
   193	                promptTokens.addAll(
   194	                        chatFormat.encodeMessage(new ChatFormat.Message(ChatFormat.Role.SYSTEM, systemMessage.text())));
   195	            } else if (msg instanceof AiMessage aiMessage) {
   196	                promptTokens.addAll(
   197	                        chatFormat.encodeMessage(new ChatFormat.Message(ChatFormat.Role.ASSISTANT, aiMessage.text())));
   198	            }
   199	        }
   200	
   201	        // EncodeHeader to prime the model to start generating a new assistant response.
   202	        promptTokens.addAll(chatFormat.encodeHeader(new ChatFormat.Message(ChatFormat.Role.ASSISTANT, "")));
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    /**
   206	     * Manually releases GPU resources allocated by TornadoVM.
   207	     *
   208	     * <p>This method can be called explicitly to free resources immediately,
   209	     * or will be called automatically when the model is garbage collected. It's safe to call this method multiple times.
   210	     */
   211	    public void freeTornadoVMGPUResources() {
   212	        if (!closed && cleanable != null) {
   213	            cleanable.clean();
   214	            closed = true;
   215	        }
   216	    }
   217	
   218	    /**
   219	     * Closes the model and releases all associated resources.
   220	     *
   221	     * <p>This method implements AutoCloseable, allowing the model to be used
   222	     * with try-with-resources statements for automatic resource management.
   223	     */
   224	    @Override
   225	    public void close() {
   226	        freeTornadoVMGPUResources();
   227	    }
   228	
   229	    /**
   230	     * Cleanup action for TornadoVM resources that holds no reference to the model instance. This prevents memory leaks while ensuring resources are properly cleaned up.
   231	     */
   232	    private static class TornadoVMCleanupAction implements Runnable {
   233	        private final TornadoVMMasterPlan plan;
   234	
   235	        TornadoVMCleanupAction(TornadoVMMasterPlan plan) {
   236	            this.plan = plan;
   237	        }
   238	
   239	        @Override
   240	        public void run() {
   241	            if (plan != null) {
   242	                try {
   243	                    plan.freeTornadoExecutionPlan();
   244	                } catch (Exception e) {
   245	                    System.err.println("Error while cleaning up TornadoVM resources: " + e.getMessage());
   246	                }
   247	            }
   248	        }
   249	    }
   250	}

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring.onnx;
     2	
     3	import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.Encoding;
     4	import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.HuggingFaceTokenizer;
     5	import ai.djl.util.PairList;
     6	import ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor;
     7	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtEnvironment;
     8	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtException;
     9	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession;
    10	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession.Result;
    11	
    12	import java.nio.file.Paths;
    13	import java.util.*;
    14	
    15	import static ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor.createTensor;
    16	
    17	class OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder {
    18	
    19	    private final OrtEnvironment environment;
    20	    private final OrtSession session;
    21	    private final Set<String> expectedInputs;
    22	    private final HuggingFaceTokenizer tokenizer;
    23	    private final boolean normalize;
    24	
    25	    public OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder(String modelPath, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength, boolean normalize) {
    26	        try {
    27	            this.environment = OrtEnvironment.getEnvironment();
    28	            this.session = this.environment.createSession(modelPath, options);
    29	            this.expectedInputs = session.getInputNames();
    30	            Map<String, String> tokenizerOptions = new HashMap<String, String>() {{
    31	                put("padding", "true");
    32	                put("truncation", "LONGEST_FIRST"); // Default maximum length limit, LONGEST-FIRST prioritizes truncating the longest part
    33	                put("modelMaxLength", String.valueOf(modelMaxLength - 2));
    34	            }};
    35	            this.normalize = normalize;
    36	            this.tokenizer = HuggingFaceTokenizer.newInstance(Paths.get(pathToTokenizer), tokenizerOptions);
    37	        } catch (Exception e) {
    38	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
    39	        }
    40	    }
    41	
    42	    static class ScoringAndTokenCount {
    43	
    44	        List<Double> scores;
    45	        int tokenCount;
    46	
    47	        ScoringAndTokenCount(List<Double> scores, int tokenCount) {
    48	            this.scores = scores;
    49	            this.tokenCount = tokenCount;
    50	        }
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    ScoringAndTokenCount scoreAll(String query, List<String> documents) {
    54	        List<Double> scores;
    55	        int tokenCount = 0;
    56	        int queryTokenCount = tokenizer.tokenize(query).size() - 2;
    57	        PairList<String, String> pairs = new PairList<>();
    58	        for (String document : documents) {
    59	            pairs.add(query, document);
    60	            tokenCount += queryTokenCount + tokenizer.tokenize(document).size() - 2; // do not count special tokens [CLS] and [SEP]
    61	        }
    62	        try (Result result = this.encode(pairs)) {
    63	            scores = this.toScore(result);
    64	        } catch (OrtException e) {
    65	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
    66	        }
    67	        return new ScoringAndTokenCount(scores, tokenCount);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    private Result encode(PairList<String, String> pairs) throws OrtException {
    71	        Encoding[] encodings = this.tokenizer.batchEncode(pairs);
    72	        long[][] inputIds = new long[encodings.length][];
    73	        long[][] attentionMask = new long[encodings.length][];
    74	        long[][] tokenTypeIds = new long[encodings.length][];
    75	
    76	        for (int i = 0; i < encodings.length; i++) {
    77	            inputIds[i] = encodings[i].getIds();
    78	            attentionMask[i] = encodings[i].getAttentionMask();
    79	            tokenTypeIds[i] = encodings[i].getTypeIds();
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        try (
    83	                OnnxTensor inputIdsTensor = createTensor(environment, inputIds);
    84	                OnnxTensor attentionMaskTensor = createTensor(environment, attentionMask);
    85	                OnnxTensor tokenTypeIdsTensor = createTensor(this.environment, tokenTypeIds);
    86	        ) {
    87	            Map<String, OnnxTensor> inputs = new HashMap<>();
    88	            inputs.put("input_ids", inputIdsTensor);
    89	            inputs.put("attention_mask", attentionMaskTensor);
    90	
    91	            if (expectedInputs.contains("token_type_ids")) {
    92	                inputs.put("token_type_ids", tokenTypeIdsTensor);
    93	            }
    94	
    95	            return session.run(inputs);
    96	        }
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    private List<Double> toScore(OrtSession.Result result) throws OrtException {
   100	        float[][] output = (float[][]) result.get(0).getValue();
   101	        List<Double> scores = new ArrayList<>();
   102	        for (float[] floats : output) {
   103	            if (normalize) {
   104	                scores.add(sigmoid(floats[0]));
   105	            } else {
   106	                scores.add((double)floats[0]);
   107	            }
   108	        }
   109	        return scores;
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    private double sigmoid(float x) {
   113	        return 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-x));
   114	    }
   115	
   116	}

package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring.onnx;

import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.Encoding;
import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.HuggingFaceTokenizer;
import ai.djl.util.PairList;
import ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor;
import ai.onnxruntime.OrtEnvironment;
import ai.onnxruntime.OrtException;
import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession;
import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession.Result;

import java.nio.file.Paths;
import java.util.*;

import static ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor.createTensor;

class OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder {

    private final OrtEnvironment environment;
    private final OrtSession session;
    private final Set<String> expectedInputs;
    private final HuggingFaceTokenizer tokenizer;
    private final boolean normalize;

    public OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder(String modelPath, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength, boolean normalize) {
        try {
            this.environment = OrtEnvironment.getEnvironment();
            this.session = this.environment.createSession(modelPath, options);
            this.expectedInputs = session.getInputNames();
            Map<String, String> tokenizerOptions = new HashMap<String, String>() {{
                put("padding", "true");
                put("truncation", "LONGEST_FIRST"); // Default maximum length limit, LONGEST-FIRST prioritizes truncating the longest part
                put("modelMaxLength", String.valueOf(modelMaxLength - 2));
            }};
            this.normalize = normalize;
            this.tokenizer = HuggingFaceTokenizer.newInstance(Paths.get(pathToTokenizer), tokenizerOptions);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            throw new RuntimeException(e);
        }
    }

    static class ScoringAndTokenCount {

        List<Double> scores;
        int tokenCount;

        ScoringAndTokenCount(List<Double> scores, int tokenCount) {
            this.scores = scores;
            this.tokenCount = tokenCount;
        }
    }

    ScoringAndTokenCount scoreAll(String query, List<String> documents) {
        List<Double> scores;
        int tokenCount = 0;
        int queryTokenCount = tokenizer.tokenize(query).size() - 2;
        PairList<String, String> pairs = new PairList<>();
        for (String document : documents) {
            pairs.add(query, document);
            tokenCount += queryTokenCount + tokenizer.tokenize(document).size() - 2; // do not count special tokens [CLS] and [SEP]
        }
        try (Result result = this.encode(pairs)) {
            scores = this.toScore(result);
        } catch (OrtException e) {
            throw new RuntimeException(e);
        }
        return new ScoringAndTokenCount(scores, tokenCount);
    }

    private Result encode(PairList<String, String> pairs) throws OrtException {
        Encoding[] encodings = this.tokenizer.batchEncode(pairs);
        long[][] inputIds = new long[encodings.length][];
        long[][] attentionMask = new long[encodings.length][];
        long[][] tokenTypeIds = new long[encodings.length][];

        for (int i = 0; i < encodings.length; i++) {
            inputIds[i] = encodings[i].getIds();
            attentionMask[i] = encodings[i].getAttentionMask();
            tokenTypeIds[i] = encodings[i].getTypeIds();
        }

        try (
                OnnxTensor inputIdsTensor = createTensor(environment, inputIds);
                OnnxTensor attentionMaskTensor = createTensor(environment, attentionMask);
                OnnxTensor tokenTypeIdsTensor = createTensor(this.environment, tokenTypeIds);
        ) {
            Map<String, OnnxTensor> inputs = new HashMap<>();
            inputs.put("input_ids", inputIdsTensor);
            inputs.put("attention_mask", attentionMaskTensor);

            if (expectedInputs.contains("token_type_ids")) {
                inputs.put("token_type_ids", tokenTypeIdsTensor);
            }

            return session.run(inputs);
        }
    }

    private List<Double> toScore(OrtSession.Result result) throws OrtException {
        float[][] output = (float[][]) result.get(0).getValue();
        List<Double> scores = new ArrayList<>();
        for (float[] floats : output) {
            if (normalize) {
                scores.add(sigmoid(floats[0]));
            } else {
                scores.add((double)floats[0]);
            }
        }
        return scores;
    }

    private double sigmoid(float x) {
        return 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-x));
    }

    /**
     * Closes the underlying ONNX Runtime session and releases all associated resources.
     * This should be called when the model is no longer needed to free native memory.
     */
    public void close() {
        try {
            this.session.close();
        } catch (OrtException e) {
            throw new RuntimeException(e);
        }
    }

}

package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring.onnx;

import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession;

public class OnnxScoringModel extends AbstractInProcessScoringModel implements AutoCloseable {

    private static final int DEFAULT_MODEL_MAX_LENGTH = 510; // 512 - 2 (special tokens [CLS] and [SEP])

    private static final boolean DEFAULT_NORMALIZE = false;

    private final OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder onnxBertBiEncoder;

    public OnnxScoringModel(String pathToModel, String pathToTokenizer) {
        this.onnxBertBiEncoder = loadFromFileSystem(pathToModel, new OrtSession.SessionOptions(), pathToTokenizer, DEFAULT_MODEL_MAX_LENGTH, DEFAULT_NORMALIZE);
    }

    public OnnxScoringModel(String pathToModel, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer) {
        this.onnxBertBiEncoder = loadFromFileSystem(pathToModel, options, pathToTokenizer, DEFAULT_MODEL_MAX_LENGTH, DEFAULT_NORMALIZE);
    }

    public OnnxScoringModel(String pathToModel, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength) {
        this.onnxBertBiEncoder = loadFromFileSystem(pathToModel, new OrtSession.SessionOptions(), pathToTokenizer, modelMaxLength, DEFAULT_NORMALIZE);
    }

    public OnnxScoringModel(String pathToModel, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength, boolean normalize) {
        this.onnxBertBiEncoder = loadFromFileSystem(pathToModel, options, pathToTokenizer, modelMaxLength, normalize);
    }

    protected OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder model() {
        return this.onnxBertBiEncoder;
    }

    /**
     * Closes the underlying ONNX Runtime session and releases all associated resources.
     * This should be called when the model is no longer needed to free native memory.
     */
    @Override
    public void close() {
        this.onnxBertBiEncoder.close();
    }
}

package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring;

import dev.langchain4j.data.segment.TextSegment;
import dev.langchain4j.model.output.Response;

import java.util.List;

import static dev.langchain4j.internal.ValidationUtils.ensureEq;
import static java.util.Collections.singletonList;

/**
 * Represents a model capable of scoring a text against a query.
 * <br>
 * Useful for identifying the most relevant texts when scoring multiple texts against the same query.
 * <br>
 * The scoring model can be employed for re-ranking purposes.
 */
public interface ScoringModel extends AutoCloseable {

    /**
     * Scores a given text against a given query.
     *
     * @param text  The text to be scored.
     * @param query The query against which to score the text.
     * @return the score.
     */
    default Response<Double> score(String text, String query) {
        return score(TextSegment.from(text), query);
    }

    /**
     * Scores a given {@link TextSegment} against a given query.
     *
     * @param segment The {@link TextSegment} to be scored.
     * @param query   The query against which to score the segment.
     * @return the score.
     */
    default Response<Double> score(TextSegment segment, String query) {
        Response<List<Double>> response = scoreAll(singletonList(segment), query);
        ensureEq(response.content().size(), 1,
                "Expected a single score, but received %d", response.content().size());
        return Response.from(response.content().get(0), response.tokenUsage(), response.finishReason());
    }

    /**
     * Scores all provided {@link TextSegment}s against a given query.
     *
     * @param segments The list of {@link TextSegment}s to score.
     * @param query    The query against which to score the segments.
     * @return the list of scores. The order of scores corresponds to the order of {@link TextSegment}s.
     */
    Response<List<Double>> scoreAll(List<TextSegment> segments, String query);

    /**
     * Closes this scoring model and releases any resources associated with it.
     * The default implementation does nothing.
     */
    @Override
    default void close() {
    }
}

OBSERVATION:

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring.onnx;
     2	
     3	import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.Encoding;
     4	import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.HuggingFaceTokenizer;
     5	import ai.djl.util.PairList;
     6	import ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor;
     7	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtEnvironment;
     8	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtException;
     9	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession;
    10	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession.Result;
    11	
    12	import java.nio.file.Paths;
    13	import java.util.*;
    14	
    15	import static ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor.createTensor;
    16	
    17	class OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder {
    18	
    19	    private final OrtEnvironment environment;
    20	    private final OrtSession session;
    21	    private final Set<String> expectedInputs;
    22	    private final HuggingFaceTokenizer tokenizer;
    23	    private final boolean normalize;
    24	
    25	    public OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder(String modelPath, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength, boolean normalize) {
    26	        try {
    27	            this.environment = OrtEnvironment.getEnvironment();
    28	            this.session = this.environment.createSession(modelPath, options);
    29	            this.expectedInputs = session.getInputNames();
    30	            Map<String, String> tokenizerOptions = new HashMap<String, String>() {{
    31	                put("padding", "true");
    32	                put("truncation", "LONGEST_FIRST"); // Default maximum length limit, LONGEST-FIRST prioritizes truncating the longest part
    33	                put("modelMaxLength", String.valueOf(modelMaxLength - 2));
    34	            }};
    35	            this.normalize = normalize;
    36	            this.tokenizer = HuggingFaceTokenizer.newInstance(Paths.get(pathToTokenizer), tokenizerOptions);
    37	        } catch (Exception e) {
    38	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
    39	        }
    40	    }
    41	
    42	    static class ScoringAndTokenCount {
    43	
    44	        List<Double> scores;
    45	        int tokenCount;
    46	
    47	        ScoringAndTokenCount(List<Double> scores, int tokenCount) {
    48	            this.scores = scores;
    49	            this.tokenCount = tokenCount;
    50	        }
    51	    }
    52	
    53	    ScoringAndTokenCount scoreAll(String query, List<String> documents) {
    54	        List<Double> scores;
    55	        int tokenCount = 0;
    56	        int queryTokenCount = tokenizer.tokenize(query).size() - 2;
    57	        PairList<String, String> pairs = new PairList<>();
    58	        for (String document : documents) {
    59	            pairs.add(query, document);
    60	            tokenCount += queryTokenCount + tokenizer.tokenize(document).size() - 2; // do not count special tokens [CLS] and [SEP]
    61	        }
    62	        try (Result result = this.encode(pairs)) {
    63	            scores = this.toScore(result);
    64	        } catch (OrtException e) {
    65	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
    66	        }
    67	        return new ScoringAndTokenCount(scores, tokenCount);
    68	    }
    69	
    70	    private Result encode(PairList<String, String> pairs) throws OrtException {
    71	        Encoding[] encodings = this.tokenizer.batchEncode(pairs);
    72	        long[][] inputIds = new long[encodings.length][];
    73	        long[][] attentionMask = new long[encodings.length][];
    74	        long[][] tokenTypeIds = new long[encodings.length][];
    75	
    76	        for (int i = 0; i < encodings.length; i++) {
    77	            inputIds[i] = encodings[i].getIds();
    78	            attentionMask[i] = encodings[i].getAttentionMask();
    79	            tokenTypeIds[i] = encodings[i].getTypeIds();
    80	        }
    81	
    82	        try (
    83	                OnnxTensor inputIdsTensor = createTensor(environment, inputIds);
    84	                OnnxTensor attentionMaskTensor = createTensor(environment, attentionMask);
    85	                OnnxTensor tokenTypeIdsTensor = createTensor(this.environment, tokenTypeIds);
    86	        ) {
    87	            Map<String, OnnxTensor> inputs = new HashMap<>();
    88	            inputs.put("input_ids", inputIdsTensor);
    89	            inputs.put("attention_mask", attentionMaskTensor);
    90	
    91	            if (expectedInputs.contains("token_type_ids")) {
    92	                inputs.put("token_type_ids", tokenTypeIdsTensor);
    93	            }
    94	
    95	            return session.run(inputs);
    96	        }
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    private List<Double> toScore(OrtSession.Result result) throws OrtException {
   100	        float[][] output = (float[][]) result.get(0).getValue();
   101	        List<Double> scores = new ArrayList<>();
   102	        for (float[] floats : output) {
   103	            if (normalize) {
   104	                scores.add(sigmoid(floats[0]));
   105	            } else {
   106	                scores.add((double)floats[0]);
   107	            }
   108	        }
   109	        return scores;
   110	    }
   111	
   112	    private double sigmoid(float x) {
   113	        return 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-x));
   114	    }
   115	
   116	    /**
   117	     * Closes the underlying ONNX Runtime session and releases all associated resources.
   118	     * This should be called when the model is no longer needed to free native memory.
   119	     */
   120	    public void close() {
   121	        try {
   122	            this.session.close();
   123	        } catch (OrtException e) {
   124	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
   125	        }
   126	    }
   127	
   128	}

     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring;
     2	
     3	import dev.langchain4j.data.segment.TextSegment;
     4	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.Response;
     5	
     6	import java.util.List;
     7	
     8	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.ValidationUtils.ensureEq;
     9	import static java.util.Collections.singletonList;
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * Represents a model capable of scoring a text against a query.
    13	 * <br>
    14	 * Useful for identifying the most relevant texts when scoring multiple texts against the same query.
    15	 * <br>
    16	 * The scoring model can be employed for re-ranking purposes.
    17	 */
    18	public interface ScoringModel extends AutoCloseable {
    19	
    20	    /**
    21	     * Scores a given text against a given query.
    22	     *
    23	     * @param text  The text to be scored.
    24	     * @param query The query against which to score the text.
    25	     * @return the score.
    26	     */
    27	    default Response<Double> score(String text, String query) {
    28	        return score(TextSegment.from(text), query);
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    /**
    32	     * Scores a given {@link TextSegment} against a given query.
    33	     *
    34	     * @param segment The {@link TextSegment} to be scored.
    35	     * @param query   The query against which to score the segment.
    36	     * @return the score.
    37	     */
    38	    default Response<Double> score(TextSegment segment, String query) {
    39	        Response<List<Double>> response = scoreAll(singletonList(segment), query);
    40	        ensureEq(response.content().size(), 1,
    41	                "Expected a single score, but received %d", response.content().size());
    42	        return Response.from(response.content().get(0), response.tokenUsage(), response.finishReason());
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    /**
    46	     * Scores all provided {@link TextSegment}s against a given query.
    47	     *
    48	     * @param segments The list of {@link TextSegment}s to score.
    49	     * @param query    The query against which to score the segments.
    50	     * @return the list of scores. The order of scores corresponds to the order of {@link TextSegment}s.
    51	     */
    52	    Response<List<Double>> scoreAll(List<TextSegment> segments, String query);
    53	
    54	    /**
    55	     * Closes this scoring model and releases any resources associated with it.
    56	     * The default implementation does nothing.
    57	     */
    58	    @Override
    59	    default void close() {
    60	    }
    61	}

2026-05-30 02:50:51,640 - DEBUG - swea-lm-langchain4j__langchain4j-4876 - Response: ModelResponse(id='42b0f4fac6d045ab9790620a9f554646', created=1780109440, model='DeepSeek-V4-Pro', object='chat.completion', system_fingerprint=None, choices=[Choices(finish_reason='tool_calls', index=0, message=Message(content="\n\nThe code compiles successfully. Now let me think about edge cases:\n\n1. **Double close**: What if `close()` is called twice? The `OrtSession.close()` should be idempotent (typically it is), but we could add a guard.\n\n2. **Using model after close**: If someone calls `scoreAll()` after `close()`, it will likely throw an exception from the ONNX runtime. That's expected behavior.\n\n3. **The `ScoringModel` interface change**: I added `extends AutoCloseable` with a default `close()` method. This is backwards compatible because:\n   - All existing implementations don't need to change anything (they get the default no-op close)\n   - `OnnxScoringModel` overrides `close()` to actually release resources\n   - The `AutoCloseable` interface means the model can be used in try-with-resources\n\nBut wait, there's a subtlety: the `AbstractInProcessScoringModel` implements `ScoringModel`, and `OnnxScoringModel` extends `AbstractInProcessScoringModel`. Since `ScoringModel` now extends `AutoCloseable` with a default `close()`, and `OnnxScoringModel` also declares `implements AutoCloseable`, there's no conflict.\n\nHowever, I realize that `OnnxScoringModel` explicitly stating `implements AutoCloseable` is redundant since it already extends `AbstractInProcessScoringModel` which implements `ScoringModel` which now extends `AutoCloseable`. But it's fine to keep it for clarity and documentation purposes. Actually, let me check if it would cause any issues...\n\nIt won't cause issues - it's just redundant but explicit. The code compiles successfully. Now let me think about edge cases:

1. **Double close**: What if `close()` is called twice? The `OrtSession.close()` should be idempotent (typically it is), but we could add a guard.

2. **Using model after close**: If someone calls `scoreAll()` after `close()`, it will likely throw an exception from the ONNX runtime. That's expected behavior.

3. **The `ScoringModel` interface change**: I added `extends AutoCloseable` with a default `close()` method. This is backwards compatible because:
   - All existing implementations don't need to change anything (they get the default no-op close)
   - `OnnxScoringModel` overrides `close()` to actually release resources
   - The `AutoCloseable` interface means the model can be used in try-with-resources

But wait, there's a subtlety: the `AbstractInProcessScoringModel` implements `ScoringModel`, and `OnnxScoringModel` extends `AbstractInProcessScoringModel`. Since `ScoringModel` now extends `AutoCloseable` with a default `close()`, and `OnnxScoringModel` also declares `implements AutoCloseable`, there's no conflict.

However, I realize that `OnnxScoringModel` explicitly stating `implements AutoCloseable` is redundant since it already extends `AbstractInProcessScoringModel` which implements `ScoringModel` which now extends `AutoCloseable`. But it's fine to keep it for clarity and documentation purposes. Actually, let me check if it would cause any issues...

It won't cause issues - it's just redundant but explicit. It's actually good practice to keep it for clarity, as users can see at a glance that `OnnxScoringModel` is `AutoCloseable`.

Let me also check if the `AbstractInProcessScoringModel` should also have a `close()` method that delegates to the model. But since it's abstract and doesn't own the encoder directly, it might not be necessary. However, we could add it for completeness.

package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring.onnx;

import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.Encoding;
import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.HuggingFaceTokenizer;
import ai.djl.util.PairList;
import ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor;
import ai.onnxruntime.OrtEnvironment;
import ai.onnxruntime.OrtException;
import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession;
import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession.Result;

import java.nio.file.Paths;
import java.util.*;

import static ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor.createTensor;

class OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder {

    private final OrtEnvironment environment;
    private final OrtSession session;
    private final Set<String> expectedInputs;
    private final HuggingFaceTokenizer tokenizer;
    private final boolean normalize;
    private boolean closed;

    public OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder(String modelPath, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength, boolean normalize) {
        try {
            this.environment = OrtEnvironment.getEnvironment();
            this.session = this.environment.createSession(modelPath, options);
            this.expectedInputs = session.getInputNames();
            Map<String, String> tokenizerOptions = new HashMap<String, String>() {{
                put("padding", "true");
                put("truncation", "LONGEST_FIRST"); // Default maximum length limit, LONGEST-FIRST prioritizes truncating the longest part
                put("modelMaxLength", String.valueOf(modelMaxLength - 2));
            }};
            this.normalize = normalize;
            this.tokenizer = HuggingFaceTokenizer.newInstance(Paths.get(pathToTokenizer), tokenizerOptions);
            this.closed = false;
        } catch (Exception e) {
            throw new RuntimeException(e);
        }
    }

    static class ScoringAndTokenCount {

        List<Double> scores;
        int tokenCount;

        ScoringAndTokenCount(List<Double> scores, int tokenCount) {
            this.scores = scores;
            this.tokenCount = tokenCount;
        }
    }

    ScoringAndTokenCount scoreAll(String query, List<String> documents) {
        List<Double> scores;
        int tokenCount = 0;
        int queryTokenCount = tokenizer.tokenize(query).size() - 2;
        PairList<String, String> pairs = new PairList<>();
        for (String document : documents) {
            pairs.add(query, document);
            tokenCount += queryTokenCount + tokenizer.tokenize(document).size() - 2; // do not count special tokens [CLS] and [SEP]
        }
        try (Result result = this.encode(pairs)) {
            scores = this.toScore(result);
        } catch (OrtException e) {
            throw new RuntimeException(e);
        }
        return new ScoringAndTokenCount(scores, tokenCount);
    }

    private Result encode(PairList<String, String> pairs) throws OrtException {
        Encoding[] encodings = this.tokenizer.batchEncode(pairs);
        long[][] inputIds = new long[encodings.length][];
        long[][] attentionMask = new long[encodings.length][];
        long[][] tokenTypeIds = new long[encodings.length][];

        for (int i = 0; i < encodings.length; i++) {
            inputIds[i] = encodings[i].getIds();
            attentionMask[i] = encodings[i].getAttentionMask();
            tokenTypeIds[i] = encodings[i].getTypeIds();
        }

        try (
                OnnxTensor inputIdsTensor = createTensor(environment, inputIds);
                OnnxTensor attentionMaskTensor = createTensor(environment, attentionMask);
                OnnxTensor tokenTypeIdsTensor = createTensor(this.environment, tokenTypeIds);
        ) {
            Map<String, OnnxTensor> inputs = new HashMap<>();
            inputs.put("input_ids", inputIdsTensor);
            inputs.put("attention_mask", attentionMaskTensor);

            if (expectedInputs.contains("token_type_ids")) {
                inputs.put("token_type_ids", tokenTypeIdsTensor);
            }

            return session.run(inputs);
        }
    }

    private List<Double> toScore(OrtSession.Result result) throws OrtException {
        float[][] output = (float[][]) result.get(0).getValue();
        List<Double> scores = new ArrayList<>();
        for (float[] floats : output) {
            if (normalize) {
                scores.add(sigmoid(floats[0]));
            } else {
                scores.add((double)floats[0]);
            }
        }
        return scores;
    }

    private double sigmoid(float x) {
        return 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-x));
    }

    /**
     * Closes the underlying ONNX Runtime session and releases all associated resources.
     * This should be called when the model is no longer needed to free native memory.
     * Safe to call multiple times.
     */
    public void close() {
        if (closed) {
            return;
        }
        try {
            this.session.close();
            this.closed = true;
        } catch (OrtException e) {
            throw new RuntimeException(e);
        }
    }

}

=== ScoringModel.java ===
     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring;
     2	
     3	import dev.langchain4j.data.segment.TextSegment;
     4	import dev.langchain4j.model.output.Response;
     5	
     6	import java.util.List;
     7	
     8	import static dev.langchain4j.internal.ValidationUtils.ensureEq;
     9	import static java.util.Collections.singletonList;
    10	
    11	/**
    12	 * Represents a model capable of scoring a text against a query.
    13	 * <br>
    14	 * Useful for identifying the most relevant texts when scoring multiple texts against the same query.
    15	 * <br>
    16	 * The scoring model can be employed for re-ranking purposes.
    17	 */
    18	public interface ScoringModel extends AutoCloseable {
    19	
    20	    /**
    21	     * Scores a given text against a given query.
    22	     *
    23	     * @param text  The text to be scored.
    24	     * @param query The query against which to score the text.
    25	     * @return the score.
    26	     */
    27	    default Response<Double> score(String text, String query) {
    28	        return score(TextSegment.from(text), query);
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    /**
    32	     * Scores a given {@link TextSegment} against a given query.
    33	     *
    34	     * @param segment The {@link TextSegment} to be scored.
    35	     * @param query   The query against which to score the segment.
    36	     * @return the score.
    37	     */
    38	    default Response<Double> score(TextSegment segment, String query) {
    39	        Response<List<Double>> response = scoreAll(singletonList(segment), query);
    40	        ensureEq(response.content().size(), 1,
    41	                "Expected a single score, but received %d", response.content().size());
    42	        return Response.from(response.content().get(0), response.tokenUsage(), response.finishReason());
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    /**
    46	     * Scores all provided {@link TextSegment}s against a given query.
    47	     *
    48	     * @param segments The list of {@link TextSegment}s to score.
    49	     * @param query    The query against which to score the segments.
    50	     * @return the list of scores. The order of scores corresponds to the order of {@link TextSegment}s.
    51	     */
    52	    Response<List<Double>> scoreAll(List<TextSegment> segments, String query);
    53	
    54	    /**
    55	     * Closes this scoring model and releases any resources associated with it.
    56	     * The default implementation does nothing.
    57	     */
    58	    @Override
    59	    default void close() {
    60	    }
    61	}

=== OnnxScoringModel.java ===
     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring.onnx;
     2	
     3	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession;
     4	
     5	public class OnnxScoringModel extends AbstractInProcessScoringModel implements AutoCloseable {
     6	
     7	    private static final int DEFAULT_MODEL_MAX_LENGTH = 510; // 512 - 2 (special tokens [CLS] and [SEP])
     8	
     9	    private static final boolean DEFAULT_NORMALIZE = false;
    10	
    11	    private final OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder onnxBertBiEncoder;
    12	
    13	    public OnnxScoringModel(String pathToModel, String pathToTokenizer) {
    14	        this.onnxBertBiEncoder = loadFromFileSystem(pathToModel, new OrtSession.SessionOptions(), pathToTokenizer, DEFAULT_MODEL_MAX_LENGTH, DEFAULT_NORMALIZE);
    15	    }
    16	
    17	    public OnnxScoringModel(String pathToModel, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer) {
    18	        this.onnxBertBiEncoder = loadFromFileSystem(pathToModel, options, pathToTokenizer, DEFAULT_MODEL_MAX_LENGTH, DEFAULT_NORMALIZE);
    19	    }
    20	
    21	    public OnnxScoringModel(String pathToModel, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength) {
    22	        this.onnxBertBiEncoder = loadFromFileSystem(pathToModel, new OrtSession.SessionOptions(), pathToTokenizer, modelMaxLength, DEFAULT_NORMALIZE);
    23	    }
    24	
    25	    public OnnxScoringModel(String pathToModel, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength, boolean normalize) {
    26	        this.onnxBertBiEncoder = loadFromFileSystem(pathToModel, options, pathToTokenizer, modelMaxLength, normalize);
    27	    }
    28	
    29	    protected OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder model() {
    30	        return this.onnxBertBiEncoder;
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    /**
    34	     * Closes the underlying ONNX Runtime session and releases all associated resources.
    35	     * This should be called when the model is no longer needed to free native memory.
    36	     */
    37	    @Override
    38	    public void close() {
    39	        this.onnxBertBiEncoder.close();
    40	    }
    41	}

=== OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder.java ===
     1	package dev.langchain4j.model.scoring.onnx;
     2	
     3	import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.Encoding;
     4	import ai.djl.huggingface.tokenizers.HuggingFaceTokenizer;
     5	import ai.djl.util.PairList;
     6	import ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor;
     7	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtEnvironment;
     8	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtException;
     9	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession;
    10	import ai.onnxruntime.OrtSession.Result;
    11	
    12	import java.nio.file.Paths;
    13	import java.util.*;
    14	
    15	import static ai.onnxruntime.OnnxTensor.createTensor;
    16	
    17	class OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder {
    18	
    19	    private final OrtEnvironment environment;
    20	    private final OrtSession session;
    21	    private final Set<String> expectedInputs;
    22	    private final HuggingFaceTokenizer tokenizer;
    23	    private final boolean normalize;
    24	    private boolean closed;
    25	
    26	    public OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder(String modelPath, OrtSession.SessionOptions options, String pathToTokenizer, int modelMaxLength, boolean normalize) {
    27	        try {
    28	            this.environment = OrtEnvironment.getEnvironment();
    29	            this.session = this.environment.createSession(modelPath, options);
    30	            this.expectedInputs = session.getInputNames();
    31	            Map<String, String> tokenizerOptions = new HashMap<String, String>() {{
    32	                put("padding", "true");
    33	                put("truncation", "LONGEST_FIRST"); // Default maximum length limit, LONGEST-FIRST prioritizes truncating the longest part
    34	                put("modelMaxLength", String.valueOf(modelMaxLength - 2));
    35	            }};
    36	            this.normalize = normalize;
    37	            this.tokenizer = HuggingFaceTokenizer.newInstance(Paths.get(pathToTokenizer), tokenizerOptions);
    38	            this.closed = false;
    39	        } catch (Exception e) {
    40	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
    41	        }
    42	    }
    43	
    44	    static class ScoringAndTokenCount {
    45	
    46	        List<Double> scores;
    47	        int tokenCount;
    48	
    49	        ScoringAndTokenCount(List<Double> scores, int tokenCount) {
    50	            this.scores = scores;
    51	            this.tokenCount = tokenCount;
    52	        }
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    ScoringAndTokenCount scoreAll(String query, List<String> documents) {
    56	        List<Double> scores;
    57	        int tokenCount = 0;
    58	        int queryTokenCount = tokenizer.tokenize(query).size() - 2;
    59	        PairList<String, String> pairs = new PairList<>();
    60	        for (String document : documents) {
    61	            pairs.add(query, document);
    62	            tokenCount += queryTokenCount + tokenizer.tokenize(document).size() - 2; // do not count special tokens [CLS] and [SEP]
    63	        }
    64	        try (Result result = this.encode(pairs)) {
    65	            scores = this.toScore(result);
    66	        } catch (OrtException e) {
    67	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
    68	        }
    69	        return new ScoringAndTokenCount(scores, tokenCount);
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    private Result encode(PairList<String, String> pairs) throws OrtException {
    73	        Encoding[] encodings = this.tokenizer.batchEncode(pairs);
    74	        long[][] inputIds = new long[encodings.length][];
    75	        long[][] attentionMask = new long[encodings.length][];
    76	        long[][] tokenTypeIds = new long[encodings.length][];
    77	
    78	        for (int i = 0; i < encodings.length; i++) {
    79	            inputIds[i] = encodings[i].getIds();
    80	            attentionMask[i] = encodings[i].getAttentionMask();
    81	            tokenTypeIds[i] = encodings[i].getTypeIds();
    82	        }
    83	
    84	        try (
    85	                OnnxTensor inputIdsTensor = createTensor(environment, inputIds);
    86	                OnnxTensor attentionMaskTensor = createTensor(environment, attentionMask);
    87	                OnnxTensor tokenTypeIdsTensor = createTensor(this.environment, tokenTypeIds);
    88	        ) {
    89	            Map<String, OnnxTensor> inputs = new HashMap<>();
    90	            inputs.put("input_ids", inputIdsTensor);
    91	            inputs.put("attention_mask", attentionMaskTensor);
    92	
    93	            if (expectedInputs.contains("token_type_ids")) {
    94	                inputs.put("token_type_ids", tokenTypeIdsTensor);
    95	            }
    96	
    97	            return session.run(inputs);
    98	        }
    99	    }
   100	
   101	    private List<Double> toScore(OrtSession.Result result) throws OrtException {
   102	        float[][] output = (float[][]) result.get(0).getValue();
   103	        List<Double> scores = new ArrayList<>();
   104	        for (float[] floats : output) {
   105	            if (normalize) {
   106	                scores.add(sigmoid(floats[0]));
   107	            } else {
   108	                scores.add((double)floats[0]);
   109	            }
   110	        }
   111	        return scores;
   112	    }
   113	
   114	    private double sigmoid(float x) {
   115	        return 1 / (1 + Math.exp(-x));
   116	    }
   117	
   118	    /**
   119	     * Closes the underlying ONNX Runtime session and releases all associated resources.
   120	     * This should be called when the model is no longer needed to free native memory.
   121	     * Safe to call multiple times.
   122	     */
   123	    public void close() {
   124	        if (closed) {
   125	            return;
   126	        }
   127	        try {
   128	            this.session.close();
   129	            this.closed = true;
   130	        } catch (OrtException e) {
   131	            throw new RuntimeException(e);
   132	        }
   133	    }
   134	
   135	}

Let me verify our changes summarize:

## Summary of Changes

### 1. `ScoringModel.java` (interface)
- Added `extends AutoCloseable` to the interface
- Added a default `close()` method with a no-op implementation, ensuring backward compatibility with all existing implementations

### 2. `OnnxScoringModel.java`
- Added `implements AutoCloseable` (explicit, though now inherited from `ScoringModel`)
- Added `close()` method that delegates to `onnxBertBiEncoder.close()`
- Added Javadoc documenting the behavior

### 3. `OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder.java`
- Added a `closed` boolean field to track whether resources have been released
- Added `close()` method that:
  - Guards against double-close via the `closed` flag
  - Calls `session.close()` to release native ONNX Runtime resources
  - Sets `closed = true` after successful closure
  - Wraps `OrtException` in `RuntimeException` for convenience
- Added Javadoc documenting the behavior

These changes ensure that:
1. `OnnxScoringModel` now implements `AutoCloseable` and can be used in try-with-resources
2. Calling `close()` properly propagates to `OrtSession.close()`, releasing non-JVM native memory
3. The `ScoringModel` interface now extends `AutoCloseable` with a default no-op `close()`, allowing all scoring models to be treated as closeable resources
4. Double-close is safe due to the guard in `OnnxScoringBertCrossEncoder`
